      function loadFile(url, success){
       if (!FileIsExt(cacheArray,url)){

        fileObj.type = "text/javascript";
        fileObj.src = url;

     importAd(ad_common_list,function(){
      var ad_type_js = [];

       ad_type_js = ad_type_js.concat(ad_type_js1);

      }

       importAd(ad_type_js,function(){
        importAd(ad_boot);
       });
      }else{
       importAd(ad_boot);
      }
     });
